Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(1): "Area of operation" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(1)(a): in the case of an authority of a city, the city, except that the area of operation of an authority of a city does not include an area that lies within the territorial boundaries of some other city; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(1)(b): in the case of an authority of a county, all of the county for which it is created except, that a county authority may not undertake a project within the boundaries of a city unless a resolution has been adopted by the governing body of the city, and by any authority which has been established and authorized to exercise its powers in the city, declaring that there is need for the county authority to exercise its powers within that city.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(2): "Blighted area" means an area where dwellings predominate that, by reason of dilapidation, overcrowding, faulty arrangement or design, lack of ventilation, light, or sanitary facilities or any combination of these factors, are detrimental to safety, health, and morals.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(3): "Bonds" means bonds, notes, interim certificates, debentures, or other obligations issued by an authority under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(4): "City" means a city or town in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(5): "Clerk" means the city or county clerk, or the officer charged with the duties customarily imposed on the clerk.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(6): "County" means a county in the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(7): "Elderly" means a person who meets the age, disability, or other conditions established by regulation of the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(8): "Federal government" includes the United States of America, the Department of Housing and Urban Development, or any other agency or instrumentality, corporate or otherwise, of the United States.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(9): "Governing body" means, in the case of a city, the council or other body of the city in which is vested legislative authority customarily imposed on the city council, and in the case of a county, the board of county commissioners.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(10): "Housing authority" or "authority" means a public body corporate and politic created by this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11): (11)(a)(i); (ii)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(a): (11)(a)(i); (ii) "Housing project" or "project" means a work or undertaking, on contiguous or noncontiguous sites to:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(a)(i): demolish, clear, or remove buildings from a blighted area;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(a)(ii): provide or assist in providing decent, safe, and sanitary urban or rural dwellings, apartments, or other living accommodations for persons of medium and low income by any suitable methods, including rental, sale of individual units in single or multifamily structures under conventional condominium, cooperative sales contract, lease-purchase agreement, loans, or subsidizing of rentals or charges; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(a)(iii): (11)(a)(i); (ii) accomplish a combination of Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b): "Housing project" includes:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(i): buildings, land, equipment, facilities, and other real or personal property for necessary, convenient, or desirable appurtenances;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(ii): streets, sewers, water service, utilities, parks, site preparation and landscaping;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(iii): facilities for administrative, community, health, recreational, welfare, or other purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(iv): the planning of the buildings and other improvements;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(v): the acquisition of property or any interest in the property;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(vi): the demolition of existing structures;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(vii): the construction, reconstruction, rehabilitation, alteration, or repair of the improvements and all other work in connection with them; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(11)(b)(viii): all other real and personal property and all tangible or intangible assets held or used in connection with the housing project.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(12): "Major disaster" means a flood, drought, fire, hurricane, earthquake, storm, or other catastrophe, which in the determination of the governing body is of sufficient severity and magnitude to warrant the use of available resources of the federal, state, and local governments to alleviate the damage, hardship, or suffering caused.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(13): "Mayor" means the mayor of the city or the officer charged with the duties customarily imposed on the mayor or executive head of a city.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(14): "Obligee of an authority" or "obligee" includes a bondholder, agent or trustee for a bondholder, a lessor demising to the authority used in connection with a project, an assignee or assignees of the lessor's interest in whole or in part, and the federal government when it is a party to a contract with the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(15): "Persons of medium and low income" mean persons or families who, as determined by the authority undertaking a project, cannot afford to pay the amounts at which private enterprise, unaided by appropriate assistance, is providing a substantial supply of decent, safe and sanitary housing.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(16): "Person with a disability" means a person with any disability as defined by and covered under the Americans with Disabilities Act of 1990, 42 U.S.C. Sec. 12102.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(17): "Public body" means a city, county or municipal corporation, commission, district, authority, agency, subdivision, or other body of the foregoing.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-401(18): "Real property" includes all lands, improvements, and fixtures on them, property of any nature appurtenant to them or used in connection with them, and every estate, interest, and right, legal or equitable, including terms for years.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402 Creation of housing authority authorized -- Procedure -- Registration as a limited purpose entity.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(1): The governing body of each public body of the state, except the state itself, may create an authority, corporate and politic, to be known as a "housing authority."
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(2): The governing body of a city or county shall give consideration to the need for an authority:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(2)(a): on its own motion; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(2)(b): upon the filing of a petition signed by 25 electors of the city or county asserting that there is need for an authority to function in the city or county and requesting that its governing body make a declaration to that effect.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(3): The governing body shall adopt a resolution declaring there is need for an authority and creating an authority in the city or county if it finds:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(3)(a): that unsanitary or unsafe inhabited dwelling accommodations exist in the city or county; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(3)(b): that there is a shortage of safe and sanitary dwelling accommodations in the city or county available to persons of medium and low income at rentals or prices they can afford.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(4): (3)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(4)(a): (3) In any suit, action, or proceeding involving the validity or enforcement of a contract of the authority, an authority shall be conclusively deemed to have become established and authorized to transact business and exercise its powers upon proof of the adoption of the resolution prescribed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(4)(b): A copy of the resolution duly certified by the clerk shall be admissible in evidence in a suit, action, or proceeding.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(5): In counties of the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth class, the governing body of each public body of the state, except the state itself, may contract with or execute an interlocal agreement for services to be provided by an existing housing authority established in another political subdivision.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(6): 67-1a-15; (6)(a); 67-1a-15; 67-3-1
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(6)(a): 67-1a-15 Each housing authority shall register and maintain the housing authority's registration as a limited purpose entity, in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-402(6)(b): (6)(a); 67-1a-15; 67-3-1 A housing authority that fails to comply with Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403 Indian housing authorities.
-----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(1)(a): There is created, with respect to each Indian tribe, band, or community in the state, a public body corporate and politic, to function in the operating area of the Indian tribe, band, or community to be known as the "housing authority" of the Indian tribe, band, or community, which is an agency of this state, possessing all powers, rights, and functions specified for city and county authorities created under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(1)(b): This Indian housing authority may not transact business or exercise its powers unless the governing council of the tribe, band, or community, by proper resolution, declares that there is a need for an authority to function for the tribe, band, or community.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(2)(a): Except as otherwise provided in this part, the provisions of law applicable to housing authorities created for cities and counties and the commissioners of these authorities shall be applicable to Indian housing authorities and the commissioners of those authorities.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-403(2)(b): The chief or other governing head of an Indian tribe, band, or community may exercise all appointing and other powers with respect to an Indian housing authority that are vested by this part in the mayor of a city relating to a city housing authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404 Commissioners -- Appointment -- Terms -- Quorum -- Meetings -- Employment of other officers and employees authorized.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(1): If a housing authority is authorized to transact business and exercise powers under this part, not less than five nor more than seven people shall be appointed as commissioners of the authority:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(1)(a): in the case of a city, by the mayor, with the advice and consent of the city's governing body; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(1)(b): in the case of a county, by the county's governing body.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(2): (2)(a); (2)(a); (b)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(2)(a): The commissioners first appointed under this part shall serve for terms of one, two, three, four, and five years, respectively, from the date of their appointment.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(2)(b): (2)(a) After the first commissioners are appointed under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(2)(c): (2)(a); (b) Notwithstanding Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(3): A commissioner qualifies by taking the official oath of office.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(4): A commissioner may not receive compensation except necessary expenses, including traveling expenses, incurred in the discharge of the commissioner's duties.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(5): A commissioner holds office until the commissioner's successor is appointed and qualified.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(6): A certificate of appointment or reappointment of a commissioner shall be:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(6)(a): filed with the authority; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(6)(b): conclusive evidence of the appointment of the commissioner.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(7): The powers of each authority are vested in the commissioners.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(8)(a): A majority of the commissioners of an authority constitutes a quorum for the purpose of conducting its business and exercising its powers and for all other purposes notwithstanding the existence of any vacancies.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(8)(b): The authority may take action upon a vote of a majority of the commissioners present, unless the bylaws of the authority require a larger number.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(9): (9)(a) Meetings of the commissioners of an authority may be held:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(9)(a): anywhere within the area of operation of the authority; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(9)(b): (9)(a) within any area not described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(10): The commissioners of an authority shall elect a chair and vice chair from the commissioners.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(11): An authority may employ an executive director, legal and technical experts, and other officers, agents, and employees, permanent and temporary, and shall determine their qualifications, duties, and compensation.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-404(12): An authority may delegate to one or more of its agents or employees any powers or duties the authority considers proper.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405 Disclosure of interest in project -- Restrictions.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(1): A commissioner, officer, or employee of an authority, who has voluntarily acquired any of the following interests, shall disclose to the commissioners of the authority, as soon as the person has knowledge of the interest, the nature and extent of the interest:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(1)(a): a present or future interest, direct or indirect, in a project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(1)(b): a present or future interest, direct or indirect, in a property included in or planned to be included in a project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(1)(c): a contract or proposed contract relating to a project; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(1)(d): any other transaction or agreement with the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(2): The commissioners shall enter the particulars of the disclosure into the minutes of the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(3): After a disclosure of interest, the commissioner, officer, or employee may participate in any discussions concerning proposed authority action on the property, contract, transaction, or agreement in which the person has an interest, but the commissioner, officer, or employee may not vote on any action proposed by the authority regarding that property, contract, transaction, or agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-405(4): Title 67, Chapter 16, Utah Public Officers' and Employees' Ethics Act Commissioners, officers, and employees of an authority are not "public officers" for purposes of


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-406 Misconduct of commissioners -- Removal.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-406(1): A commissioner of an authority may be removed by the mayor or, in the case of an authority for a county, by the body that appointed the commissioner for inefficiency, neglect of duty, or misconduct in office.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-406(2): A commissioner may be removed only after a hearing and after having been given a copy of the charges at least 10 days prior to the hearing and having an opportunity to be heard in person or by counsel.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-406(3): If a commissioner is removed, a record of the proceedings, together with the charges and findings, shall be filed in the office of the clerk.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407 Powers of housing authority.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(1): An authority has perpetual succession and all the powers necessary to carry out the purposes of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2): An authority may:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(a): sue and be sued;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(b): have a seal and alter it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(c): make and execute contracts and other instruments necessary to the exercise of its powers;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(d): make, amend, and repeal bylaws and rules;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(e): within its area of operation, prepare, carry out, and operate projects and provide for the acquisition, construction, reconstruction, rehabilitation, improvement, extension, alteration or repair of any project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(f): undertake and carry out studies and analyses of housing needs within its area of operation and ways of meeting those needs, including data with respect to population and family groups and its distribution according to income groups, the amount and quality of available housing, including accessible housing, and its distribution according to rentals and sales prices, employment, wages and other factors affecting the local housing needs and meeting these needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(g): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(g)(i): make the results of studies and analyses available to the public and the building, housing, and supply industries; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(g)(ii): engage in research and disseminate information on housing programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(h): utilize, contract with, act through, assist, and cooperate or deal with any person, agency, institution, or organization, public or private, for the provision of services, privileges, works, or facilities, or in connection with its projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(i): notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in this part or in any other provision of law:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(i)(i): agree to any conditions attached to federal financial assistance relating to the determination of prevailing salaries or wages or payment of not less than prevailing salaries or wages or compliance with labor standards in the development or administration of projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(i)(ii): include in any contract awarded or entered into in connection with a project stipulations requiring that the contractor and all subcontractors comply with requirements as to minimum salaries or wages and maximum hours of labor; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(i)(iii): comply with any conditions attached to the financial aid of the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(j): lease, rent, sell, or lease with the option to purchase any dwellings, lands, buildings, structures, or facilities embraced in a project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(k): subject to the limitations contained in this part with respect to the rental or charges for dwellings in housing projects, establish and revise the rents or charges for the dwellings;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(l): own, hold, and improve real or personal property;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(m): purchase, lease, obtain options upon, acquire by gift, grant, bequest, devise, or otherwise any real or personal property or any interest in it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(n): sell, lease, exchange, transfer, assign, pledge, or dispose of real or personal property or any interest in it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(o): make loans for the provision of housing for occupancy by persons of medium and low income;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(p): make loans or grants for the development and construction of accessible housing;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(q): insure or provide for the insurance, in stock or mutual companies, of real or personal property or operations of the authority against any risks or hazards;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(r): procure or agree to the procurement of government insurance or guarantees of the payment of any bonds, in whole or in part, issued by the authority, including the power to pay premiums on the insurance;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(s): invest money held in reserves, sinking funds, or any funds not required for immediate disbursement in property or securities in which savings banks may legally invest money subject to their control;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(t): redeem its bonds at the redemption price established or purchase its bonds at less than redemption price, with all bonds that are redeemed or purchased to be canceled;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(u): within its area of operation, determine where blighted areas exist or where there is unsafe, insanitary, or overcrowded housing;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(v): make studies and recommendations relating to the problem of clearing, replanning, and reconstructing blighted areas, and the problem of eliminating unsafe, insanitary, or overcrowded housing and providing dwelling accommodations and maintaining a wholesome living environment for persons of medium and low income, and cooperate with any public body or the private sector in action taken in connection with those problems;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(w): acting through one or more commissioners or other persons designated by the authority, conduct examinations and investigations and hear testimony and take proof under oath at public or private hearings on any matter material for its information;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(x): administer oaths, issue subpoenas requiring the attendance of witnesses or the production of books and papers, and issue commissions for the examination of witnesses outside the state who are unable to appear before the authority or are excused from attendance;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(y): make available to appropriate agencies, including those charged with the duty of abating or requiring the correction of nuisances or like conditions or of demolishing unsafe or insanitary structures within its area of operation, its findings and recommendations with regard to any building or property where conditions exist that are dangerous to the public health, morals, safety, or welfare; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(2)(z): exercise all or any part or combination of the powers granted under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(3): (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(3)(a): If there are two or more housing authorities established within a county of the first or second class, then those housing authorities shall create a uniform online application for the housing choice voucher program with links to each of the housing authorities within the county.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(3)(b): (3)(a) As used in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-407(4): No provision of law with respect to the acquisition, operation, or disposition of property by other public bodies is applicable to an authority unless the Legislature specifically states that it is.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408 Profit from projects prohibited -- Criteria for determining rentals and payments.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(1): To accomplish the public, governmental, and charitable purposes of this part, the Legislature declares that:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(1)(a): an authority manage and operate the authority's housing projects in an efficient manner to enable each housing project to provide decent, safe, and sanitary dwelling accommodations for persons of medium and low income and fix the rentals or payments for these accommodations for persons of low income at low rates; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(1)(b): an authority may not be operated as a source of revenue to the city or county.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(2): An authority shall fix the rentals or payments for dwellings in the authority's projects at no higher rates than the authority finds necessary in order to produce revenues that, together with all other available money, revenues, income, and receipts of the authority from whatever sources derived, including federal financial assistance necessary to maintain the low-rent character of the projects, is sufficient to:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(2)(a): pay, as they become due, the principal and interest on the bonds of the authority;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(2)(b): create and maintain reserves required to assure the payment of principal and interest as it becomes due on its bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(2)(c): meet the cost of, and provide for, maintaining and operating the projects, including necessary reserves and the cost of any insurance, and the administrative expenses of the authority; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(2)(d): make payments in lieu of taxes and, after payment in full of all obligations for which federal annual contributions are pledged, make repayments of federal and local contributions as it determines are consistent with the maintenance of the low-rent character of projects.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(3): Rentals or payments for dwellings shall be established and the projects administered, in so far as possible, to assure that any federal financial assistance required is strictly limited to amounts and periods necessary to maintain the low-rent character of the projects.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(4): Nothing in this section limits the amount an authority may charge for nondwelling facilities.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-408(5): All income and revenue described in this section shall be used in the operation of the projects to aid in accomplishing the public, governmental, and charitable purposes of this part.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-409 Eligibility requirements for occupants -- Rights of obligee on default of authority.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-409(1): An authority shall make rules establishing eligibility requirements consistent with the purposes and objectives of this part for admission to and continued occupancy in its projects.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-409(2): 35A-8-408; 35A-8-408 Nothing contained in this section or in Section


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410 Penalties for fraudulently obtaining or continuing to receive housing assistance benefits.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1): A person may not knowingly, by misrepresentation, impersonation, or other fraudulent means, make a false statement to housing authority personnel or, after being accepted as a recipient of housing authority benefits, fail to disclose to housing authority personnel any:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(a): change in household composition;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(b): employment change;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(c): change in marital status;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(d): receipt of any other monetary assistance;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(e): receipt of in-kind gifts; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(1)(f): other material fact or change in circumstances that would affect the determination of that person's eligibility to receive housing assistance benefits, or would affect the amount of benefits for which the person is eligible.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(2): (1) A person may not fail to disclose any of the information described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(3): A person who has duties relating to the administration of a housing authority program may not fraudulently misappropriate funds or other assistance with which the person has been entrusted, or of which the person has gained possession by virtue of the person's position.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(4): A person may not knowingly:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(4)(a): file or falsify a claim, report, or document required by state or federal law, or provider agreement, to obtain or attempt to obtain unauthorized housing assistance benefits under this part; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(4)(b): attempt to commit, or aid or abet the commission of, an act prohibited by this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(5): The punishment for violation of a provision of this section by a housing assistance recipient is determined by the cumulative value of the money or other benefits the person received from all instances of fraud committed by the person, and not by each separate instance of fraud.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(6): The punishment for the offenses of this section are:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(6)(a): a second degree felony if the value of the funds or other benefits received, misappropriated, claimed, or applied for, is equal to or exceeds $5,000;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(6)(b): a third degree felony if the value of the funds or other benefits received, misappropriated, claimed, or applied for, is equal to or greater than $1,500 but less than $5,000;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(6)(c): a class A misdemeanor if the value of the funds or other benefits received, misappropriated, claimed, or applied for, is equal to or greater than $500 but less than $1,500; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-410(6)(d): a class B misdemeanor if the value of the funds or other benefits received, misappropriated, claimed, or applied for, is less than $500.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-411 Authorities may join or cooperate.
------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-411(1): Two or more authorities may cooperate with one another or jointly exercise any or all of their powers for the purpose of financing, issuing bonds and other obligations and giving security for them, planning, undertaking, owning, constructing, operating, or contracting with respect to a housing project or projects located within the area of operation of any one or more of the authorities.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-411(2): For this purpose, an authority may by resolution authorize a housing authority joining or cooperating with the authority to act on the authority's behalf.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-412 Preference for elderly and persons with a disability.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-412(1): For the purpose of increasing the supply of low-rent housing and related facilities for medium and low-income elderly and medium and low-income persons with a disability, an authority may exercise any of its powers under this part in projects involving dwelling accommodations designed specifically for these persons.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-412(2): For dwelling units in any projects suitable to the needs of the elderly or persons with a disability, special preference may be extended in admission to those dwelling units to these persons of medium and low income.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-413 Victims of major disaster.
----------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-413(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-413(1)(a): Notwithstanding the provisions of this or any other law relating to rentals, preferences, or eligibility for admission or occupancy of dwellings in housing projects during the period an authority determines that there is an acute need for housing to assure the availability of dwellings for victims of a major disaster, the authority may undertake the development and administration of housing projects for the federal government.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-413(1)(b): Dwellings in any housing project under the jurisdiction of the authority may be made available to victims of a major disaster.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-413(2): An authority may contract with the federal government or a public body for advance payment or reimbursement for the furnishing of housing to victims of a major disaster, including the furnishing of housing free of charge to needy disaster victims during any period covered by a determination of acute need by the authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414 Property and funds of authority declared public property -- Exemption from taxes -- Alternative agreement with public body.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(1): The property and funds of an authority are declared to be public property used for essential public, governmental, and charitable purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(2): (2)(b); (c)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(2)(a): (2)(b); (c) Subject to Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(2)(b): This tax exemption does not apply to any portion of a project used for a profit-making enterprise.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(2)(c): In taxing these portions appropriate allowance shall be made for any expenditure by an authority for utilities or other public services it provides to serve the property.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-414(3): In lieu of taxes on its exempt property an authority may agree to make payments to a public body if the authority finds that making the payments is consistent with the maintenance of the low-rent character of housing projects and the achievement of the purposes of this  part.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-415 Projects subject to local building regulations.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
A project of an authority is subject to the planning, zoning, sanitary, and building laws, ordinances, and regulations applicable to the locality in which the project is situated.

Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416 Bonds authorized -- Payment -- Security -- Liability -- Purpose -- Exemption from taxes except corporate franchise tax.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1): An authority may:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(a): issue bonds for any of its corporate purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(b): issue refunding bonds for the purpose of paying or retiring bonds previously issued by it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(c): issue bonds on which the principal and interest are payable:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(c)(i): exclusively from the income and revenues of the project financed with the proceeds of the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(c)(ii): exclusively from the income and revenues of certain designated projects, whether or not they are financed in whole or in part with the proceeds of the bonds; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(1)(c)(iii): from its revenues generally.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(2): Bonds issued by the authority may be additionally secured by a pledge of any loan, grant, or contributions, in whole or in part, from the federal government or other source, or a pledge of any income or revenues of the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(3): The members of an authority and a person executing the bonds are not liable personally on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(4)(a): The bonds and other obligations of an authority are not a debt of the city, county, state, or a political subdivision, and do not constitute indebtedness for purposes of any constitutional or statutory debt limitation or restrictions.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(4)(b): A bond or other obligation of an authority shall include a statement on the face of the bond or other obligation that explains that the bond or other obligation is not a debt of the city, county, state, or a political subdivision, and does not constitute indebtedness for purposes of any constitutional or statutory debt limitation or restrictions.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(5): The city, county, state, or political subdivision is not liable on the bonds or other obligations.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(6): These bonds or obligations may not be payable out of funds or properties other than those of the authority.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(7): Bonds of an authority are declared to be issued for an essential public and governmental purpose and to be public instrumentalities and, together with interest and income, are exempt from all taxes, except the corporate franchise tax.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-416(8): The provisions of this part exempting from taxation the properties of an authority and its bonds and interests and income on them are part of the contract for the security of bonds and have the force of contract, by virtue of this part and without the necessity of this being restated in the bonds, between the bondholders, including all transferees of the bonds, on the one hand and an authority and the state on the other.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417 Bonds to be authorized by resolution -- Form -- Sale -- Negotiability -- Validity presumed.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1): Bonds of an authority are authorized by resolution, may be issued in one or more series, and shall as provided by the resolution or its trust indenture:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(a): bear dates, including maturity dates;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(b): bear interest rates;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(c): be in denominations;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(d): be either coupon or registered;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(e): carry conversion or registration privileges;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(f): have rank or priority;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(g): be executed;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(h): be payable; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(1)(i): be subject to terms of redemption with or without premium.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(2)(a): The bonds may bear interest at a variable interest rate as provided by the resolution.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(2)(b): The resolution may establish a method, formula, or index to determine the current interest rate on the bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3): In connection with the bonds, the authority may authorize and enter into agreements or other arrangements with financial, banking, and other institutions for:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(a): letters of credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(b): standby letters of credit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(c): surety bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(d): reimbursement agreements;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(e): remarketing agreements;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(f): indexing agreements;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(g): tender agent agreements; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(h): other agreements with respect to:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(h)(i): securing the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(h)(ii): enhancing the marketability and creditworthiness of the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(h)(iii): determining a variable interest rate on the bonds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(3)(h)(iv): the payment from any legally available source, including proceeds of the bonds, fees, charges, or other amounts coming due from the agreements.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(4): As provided by resolution, the bonds may be sold at a public or private sale at par value, in excess of par value, or below par value.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(5): If a member or an officer of an authority whose signature appears on a bond or coupon ceases to be a member or an officer before the delivery of the bond or coupon, the signature is valid and sufficient for all purposes.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(6): A bond issued under this part is fully negotiable.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-417(7): In a suit, action, or proceeding involving the validity or enforceability of a bond of an authority or the security for it, a bond reciting in substance that it has been issued by the authority to aid in financing a project is conclusively considered to have been issued for that purpose, and the project is conclusively considered to have been planned, located, and carried out in accordance with this part.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418 Bonds and other obligations -- Additional powers of authority.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
In connection with the issuance of bonds or the incurring of obligations under leases and in order to secure the payment of bonds or obligations, an authority may:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(1): pledge all or a part of its gross or net rents, fees, or revenues to which its right currently exists or will accrue;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(2): mortgage all or a part of its real or personal property owned or acquired;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(3): covenant against pledging all or a part of its rents, fees, and revenues, or against mortgaging all or a part of its real or personal property to which its right or title then exists or will accrue, or against permitting or suffering any lien on the revenues or property;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(4): covenant with respect to limitations on its right to sell, lease, or otherwise dispose of any housing project and covenant as to what other, or additional debts or obligations may be incurred by it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(5): covenant as to bonds to be issued and as to the issuance of bonds in escrow or otherwise, and as to the use and disposition of the bond proceeds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(6): provide for the replacement of lost, destroyed, or mutilated bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(7): covenant against extending the time for the payment of its bonds or interest on them;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(8): covenant for the redemption of the bonds and provide the terms and conditions for them;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(9): covenant, subject to the limitations contained in this part as to the rents and fees to be charged in the operation of a housing project, the amount to be raised each year or other period of time by rents, fees, and other revenues, and as to the use and disposition of the revenues;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(10): authorize the creation of special funds for money held for construction or operating costs, debt service, reserves, or other purposes, and covenant as to the use and disposition of the money held in those funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(11): prescribe the procedure by which the terms of a contract with bondholders may be amended or abrogated, the proportion of outstanding bonds which must consent to the action, and the manner in which consent shall be given;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(12): covenant as to the use, maintenance, and replacement of any or all of its real or personal property, the insurance to be carried on it, and the use and disposition of insurance money;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(13): covenant as to the rights, liabilities, powers, and duties arising upon breach by it of a covenant, condition, or obligation;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(14): covenant and prescribe as to events of default and terms and conditions upon which any or all of its bonds or obligations shall become or may be declared due before maturity, and as to the terms and conditions upon which such declaration and its consequences may be waived;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(15): vest in an obligee of the authority, or a specified proportion of them, the right to enforce the payment of bonds or any covenants securing or relating to the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(16): vest an obligee with the right after default by the authority to take possession of and use, operate, and manage any project or any part of it or any funds connected with them, collect the rents and revenues arising from them, and dispose of them in accordance with the agreement with the authority;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(17): provide the powers and duties of an obligee and limit the obligee's liabilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(18): provide the terms and conditions upon which an obligee may enforce any covenant or rights securing or relating to the bonds;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(19): exercise all or any part or combination of the powers granted and make any covenants in addition to the covenants expressly authorized in this section;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(20): do any acts necessary, convenient, or desirable to secure its bonds; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-418(21): make any covenants or do any acts calculated to make the bonds more marketable.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-419 Issuance of bonds -- Other laws not to apply.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-419(1): This part constitutes full authority for the authorization and issuance of bonds.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-419(2): No other law for the authorization or issuance of obligations or the deposit of their proceeds that requires a bond election or in any way impedes or restricts the carrying out of the acts authorized to be done shall be construed as applying to any proceedings taken or acts done under this part.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-420 Rights of obligees of authority.
----------------------------------------------------------------
An obligee of an authority, in addition to all other rights conferred on the obligee subject to any contractual restrictions binding upon the obligee, may:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-420(1): compel an authority, its officers, agents, or employees to perform each term, provision, and covenant contained in a contract of the authority for the benefit of the obligee and to require the carrying out of all covenants and agreements of the authority and the fulfillment of all duties imposed upon it by this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-420(2): enjoin any acts or things that may be unlawful, or the violation of any of the rights of an obligee of the authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421 Obligees -- Additional rights conferred by authority.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(1): An authority may by resolution, trust indenture, mortgage, lease, or other contract, confer upon an obligee the right, in addition to all rights that may otherwise be conferred, upon default as defined in a resolution or instrument, by suit, action, or proceeding in a court of competent jurisdiction to:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(1)(a): cause possession of a project, in whole or in part, to be surrendered to the obligee;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(1)(b): obtain the appointment of a receiver of a project, in whole or in part, and of the rents and profits from the project; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(1)(c): require the authority and its officers, agents, and employees to account as if they were the trustees of an express trust.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2): The receiver:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2)(a): may enter and take possession of the project or any part of it;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2)(b): may operate and maintain the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2)(c): may collect and receive all fees, rents, revenues, or other charges arising from the project;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2)(d): shall keep the money collected from the project in a separate account; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-421(2)(e): shall use the money in accordance with the obligations of the authority as the court directs.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422 Property of authority exempt from levy and sale -- Obligees excepted -- Waiver.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(1)(a): Property, including money, acquired or held by an authority under this part shall be exempt from levy and sale by virtue of an execution.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(1)(b): An execution or other judicial process may not issue against the property.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(1)(c): A judgment against the authority is not a charge or lien upon the property.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(2): This section does not apply to or limit the right of an obligee to pursue a remedy for the enforcement of a pledge or lien given by the authority on its rents, fees, or revenues or the right of the federal government to pursue a remedy conferred upon it under this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-422(3): An authority may waive its exemption with respect to claims against a profit-making enterprise occupying a portion of a project if that waiver does not affect or impair the rights of any obligee of the authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423 Financial assistance from federal government permitted.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(1): (1)(a); (b) In addition to the powers conferred upon an authority by other provisions of this part, an authority  may:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(1)(a): borrow money or accept contributions, grants, or other financial assistance from the federal government in aid of a project or related activity concerning health, welfare, economic, educational, environmental, or related issues faced by persons of medium and low income;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(1)(b): take over, lease, or manage a project or undertaking constructed or owned by the federal government; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(1)(c): (1)(a); (b) comply with conditions and enter into contracts, covenants, mortgages, trust indentures, leases, or agreements considered necessary, convenient, or desirable to accomplish the purposes of Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(2): (2)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(2)(a): The purpose and intent of this part is to authorize an authority to do everything necessary or desirable to secure the financial aid or cooperation of the federal government in the provision of decent, safe, and sanitary dwellings and maintaining a wholesome living environment for persons of medium and low income.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-423(2)(b): (2)(a) To accomplish the purpose of Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-424 Defaults -- Conveyance of title to federal government.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-424(1): In a contract with the federal government for annual contributions, the authority may obligate itself to convey to the federal government possession of or title to the project upon the occurrence of a substantial default, as defined in the contract, with respect to the covenants and conditions to which the authority is subject.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-424(2): This obligation is specifically enforceable and does not constitute a mortgage, notwithstanding any other laws.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-424(3): In case of conveyance, the federal government may complete, operate, manage, lease, convey, or otherwise deal with the project and funds in accordance with the terms of the contract if the contract by its terms requires the federal government, as soon as practicable after it is satisfied that all defaults have been cured and that the project will be operated in accordance with the contract, to reconvey the project to the authority.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425 Powers of public body aiding in project.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1): For the purpose of aiding and cooperating in the planning, undertaking, construction, or operation of projects located within its jurisdiction, a public body may, with or without consideration:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(a): dedicate, sell, convey, or lease any of its interest in property, or grant easements, licenses, or other rights or privileges to a housing authority or the federal government;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(b): cause parks, playgrounds, recreational, community, educational, water, sewer, or drainage facilities, or other works that it is otherwise empowered to undertake to be furnished adjacent to or in connection with these projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(c): furnish, dedicate, close, pave, install, grade, regrade, plan or replan streets, roads, roadways, alleys, sidewalks, or other places that it is otherwise empowered to undertake;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(d): plan or replan, zone or rezone any parts of the public body, make exceptions from building regulations and ordinances, and make changes in its map;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(e): cause the same services to be furnished to a housing authority that the public body may furnish, and provide facilities and services, including feeding facilities and services for tenants, in connection with housing projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(f): enter into agreements with respect to the exercise by the public body of its powers relating to the repair, improvement, condemnation, closing, or demolition of unsafe, insanitary, or unfit buildings;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(g): notwithstanding the provisions of any other law, use any money belonging to or within the control of the public body, including money derived from the sale or furnishing of property or facilities to a housing authority, in the purchase of the bonds or other obligations of a housing authority and exercise any related rights;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(h): do any and all things necessary or convenient to aid and cooperate in the planning, undertaking, construction, or operation of any projects;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(i): incur the entire expense of public improvements made by a public body in exercising the powers granted in this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(1)(j): enter into agreements, that may extend over any period notwithstanding any provision or rule of law to the contrary, with a housing authority respecting action to be taken by a public body under any of the powers granted by this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(2): (1)(j) If title to or possession of a project is held by a public governmental agency authorized by law to engage in the development or administration of low-rent housing or slum clearance projects, including an agency or instrumentality of the United States, the provisions of the agreements entered into under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-425(3): A sale, conveyance, lease, or agreement provided for in this section may be made by a public body without appraisal, public notice, advertisement, or public bidding, notwithstanding any other laws to the contrary.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-426 Agreement by public body to accept payment from authority in lieu of taxes.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
In connection with a project of a housing authority located wholly or partly within the area in which a public body is authorized to act, the public body may agree with the housing authority with respect to the payment by the authority of sums in lieu of taxes for any year or period of years that are determined by the authority to be consistent with the maintenance of the low-rent character of housing projects or the achievement of the purposes of this part.

Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427 Public body may provide financial aid.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
In addition to other aids provided, a public body may provide financial aid to a housing authority by:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427(1): loan, donation, grant, contribution, and appropriation of money;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427(2): abatement or remission of taxes;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427(3): payments in lieu of taxes;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427(4): other charges; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-427(5): other means.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428 Investment in authority authorized.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428(1): The state, public officers, political subdivisions, public bodies, banks, bankers, trust companies, savings banks and institutions, building and loan associations, savings and loan associations, investment companies, insurance companies, insurance associations, other persons carrying on a banking or insurance business, executors, administrators, guardians, trustees, and other fiduciaries may legally invest money or funds belonging to them or within their control in any bonds or other obligations issued by a housing authority created under this part or issued by a public housing authority or agency in the United States, a United States Territory, the District of Columbia, Puerto Rico, Guam, or the Virgin Islands.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428(2): These bonds or other obligations shall be secured by a pledge of annual contributions or other financial assistance to be paid by the United States government or any of its agencies, or by an agreement between the United States government or any of its agencies and the public housing authority or agency in which the United States government or its agency agrees to lend to the public housing authority or agency, prior to the maturity of the bonds or other obligations, money in an amount which, together with any other money irrevocably committed to the payment of interest on the bonds or other obligations, will suffice to pay the principal of the bonds or other obligations with interest to maturity.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428(3): The money, under the terms of the agreement, is required to be used for this purpose, and the bonds and other obligations are authorized security for all public deposits and are fully negotiable in this state.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428(4): Nothing contained in this section relieves a person, firm, or corporation from any duty of exercising reasonable care in selecting securities.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-428(5): The provisions of this section apply notwithstanding any restrictions on investments contained in other laws.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429 Annual report -- Budget -- Minutes.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(1): At least once a year, an authority shall file with the clerk, with a copy given to the governing body, a report containing:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(1)(a): its activities for the preceding year;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(1)(b): its approved annual budget; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(1)(c): recommendations for legislation or other action considered necessary to carry out the purposes of this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(2): An authority shall post electronically for public review its:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(2)(a): annual approved budget; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-429(2)(b): minutes of all open meetings held by its board of commissioners.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-430 Provisions controlling -- Acts of governmental bodies deemed administrative.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-430(1): The provisions of this part are controlling, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in any other law of this state, city charter, or local ordinance.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-430(2): An action of a city, county, or governing body in carrying out the purposes of this part, whether by resolution, ordinance, or otherwise, is considered administrative in character, and no public notice or publication is required with respect to that action.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(1): "Affordable housing" means housing occupied or reserved for occupancy by households whose incomes are at or below certain income requirements at rental rates affordable to such households.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(2): "Board" means the Housing Board created by this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(3): "Fund" means the Olene Walker Housing Loan Fund created by this part.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(a): "Housing sponsor" means a person who constructs, develops, rehabilitates, purchases, or owns a housing development that is or will be subject to legally enforceable restrictive covenants that require the housing development to provide, at least in part, affordable housing.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b): "Housing sponsor" may include:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(i): a local public body;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(ii): a nonprofit, limited profit, or for profit corporation;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(iii): a limited partnership;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(iv): a limited liability company;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(v): a joint venture;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(vi): a subsidiary of the Utah Housing Corporation;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(vii): a cooperative;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(viii): a mutual housing organization;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(ix): a local government;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(x): a local housing authority;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(xi): a regional or statewide nonprofit housing or assistance organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(4)(b)(xii): any other entity that helps provide affordable housing.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-501(5): "Rural" means a county in the state other than Utah, Salt Lake, Davis, or Weber.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502 Creation and administration.
------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(1)(a): There is created an enterprise fund known as the Olene Walker Housing Loan Fund, administered by the executive director or the executive director's designee.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(1)(b): The department is the administrator of the fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(2): There shall be deposited into the fund:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(2)(a): grants, paybacks, bonuses, entitlements, and other money received by the department from the federal government to preserve, rehabilitate, build, restore, or renew housing or for other activities authorized by the fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(2)(b): transfers, grants, gifts, bequests, and money made available from any source to implement this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(2)(c): money appropriated to the fund by the Legislature.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-502(3): Title 51, Chapter 7, State Money Management Act The money in the fund shall be invested by the state treasurer according to the procedures and requirements of


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503 Housing loan fund board -- Duties -- Expenses.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(1): There is created the Olene Walker Housing Loan Fund Board.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2): The board is composed of 13 voting members.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a): The governor shall appoint the following members to four-year terms:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(i): two members from local governments, of which:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(i)(A): one member shall be a locally elected official who resides in a county of the first or second class; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(i)(B): one member shall be a locally elected official who resides in a county of the third, fourth, fifth, or sixth class;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(ii): two members from the mortgage lending community, of which:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(ii)(A): one member shall have expertise in single-family mortgage lending; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(ii)(B): one member shall have expertise in multi-family mortgage lending;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(iii): one member from real estate sales interests;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(iv): two members from home builders interests, of which:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(iv)(A): one member shall have expertise in single-family residential construction; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(iv)(B): one member shall have expertise in multi-family residential construction;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(v): one member from rental housing interests;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(vi): two members from housing advocacy interests, of which:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(vi)(A): one member who resides within any area in a county of the first or second class; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(vi)(B): one member who resides within any area in a county of the third, fourth, fifth, or sixth class;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(vii): one member of the manufactured housing interest;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(viii): one member with expertise in transit-oriented developments; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(a)(ix): one member who represents rural interests.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(b): The director or the director's designee serves as the secretary of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(2)(c): The members of the board shall annually elect a chair from among the voting membership of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(3): (2)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(3)(a): (2) Notwithstanding the requirements of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(3)(b): When a vacancy occurs in the membership for any reason, the replacement is appointed for the unexpired term.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4): Title 52, Chapter 4, Open and Public Meetings Act
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(a): Title 52, Chapter 4, Open and Public Meetings Act The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(a)(i): meet regularly, at least quarterly to conduct business of the board, on dates fixed by the board;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(a)(ii): meet twice per year, with at least one of the meetings in a rural area of the state, to provide information to and receive input from the public regarding the state's housing policies and needs;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(a)(iii): keep minutes of its meetings; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(a)(iv): Title 52, Chapter 4, Open and Public Meetings Act comply with the procedures and requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(4)(b): Seven members of the board constitute a quorum, and the governor, the chair, or a majority of the board may call a meeting of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(5): The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(5)(a): review the housing needs in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-503(5)(b): determine the relevant operational aspects of any grant, loan, or revenue collection program established under the authority of this chapter;

Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5 Low-income ADU loan guarantee pilot program.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1): 10-9a-103 As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(a): 10-9a-103 "Accessory dwelling unit" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(b): "Borrower" means a residential property owner who receives a low-income ADU loan from a lender.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(c): "Lender" means a trust company, savings bank, savings and loan association, bank, credit union, or any other entity that provides low-income ADU loans directly to borrowers.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(d): "Low-income ADU loan" means a loan made by a lender to a borrower for the purpose of financing the construction of an accessory dwelling unit that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(d)(i): located on the borrower's residential property; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(d)(ii): rented to a low-income individual.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(e): "Low-income individual" means an individual whose household income is less than 80% of the area median income.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(1)(f): "Pilot program" means the two-year pilot program created in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(2): The executive director shall establish a two-year pilot program to provide loan guarantees on behalf of borrowers for the purpose of insuring the repayment of low-income ADU loans.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3): (3)(c); (3)(c); (3)(a)(ii); (3)(a)(ii) The executive director may not provide a loan guarantee for a low-income ADU loan under the pilot program unless:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a): (3)(c); (3)(c) the lender:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(i): agrees in writing to participate in the pilot program;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(ii): makes available to prospective borrowers the option of receiving a low-income ADU loan that:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(ii)(A): has a term of 15 years; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(ii)(B): charges interest at a fixed rate;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iii): (3)(c) monitors the activities of the borrower on a yearly basis during the term of the loan to ensure the borrower's compliance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iii)(A): (3)(c) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iii)(B): any other term or condition of the loan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iv): (3)(c) promptly notifies the executive director in writing if the borrower fails to comply with:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iv)(A): (3)(c) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(a)(iv)(B): any other term or condition of the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(b): (3)(a)(ii); (3)(a)(ii) the loan terms of the low-income ADU loan:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(b)(i): (3)(a)(ii) are consistent with the loan terms described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(b)(ii): (3)(a)(ii) if different from the loan terms described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c): the borrower:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(i): agrees in writing to participate in the pilot program;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(ii): constructs an accessory dwelling unit on the borrower's residential property within one year after the day on which the borrower receives the loan;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iii): occupies the primary residence to which the accessory dwelling unit is associated:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iii)(A): after the accessory dwelling unit is completed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iii)(B): for the remainder of the term of the loan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iv): rents the accessory dwelling unit to a low-income individual:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iv)(A): after the accessory dwelling unit is completed; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(3)(c)(iv)(B): for the remainder of the term of the loan.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(4): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act; (3) At the direction of the board, the executive director shall make rules in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(4)(a): the minimum criteria for lenders and borrowers to participate in the pilot program;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-8-504.5(4)(b): (3) the terms and conditions for loan guarantees provided under the pilot program, consistent with Subsection
