Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602 COVID-19 Homeless Housing and Services Grant Program.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(1): There is established the COVID-19 Homeless Housing and Services Grant Program, a competitive grant program administered by the office and funded in accordance with 42 U.S.C. Sec. 802.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2): (2)(a)(i) The office shall distribute money to fund one or more projects that:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a): (2)(a)(i) include affordable housing units for households:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(i): whose income is no more than 30% of the area median income for households of the same size in the county or municipality where the project is located;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii): (2)(a)(i) at rental rates no greater than 30% of the income described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(A): one person if the unit is an efficiency unit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(B): two people if the unit is a one-bedroom unit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(C): four people if the unit is a two-bedroom unit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(D): five people if the unit is a three-bedroom unit;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(E): six people if the unit is a four-bedroom unit; or
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(ii)(F): eight people if the unit is a five-bedroom or larger unit; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(a)(iii): that have been impacted by the COVID-19 emergency in accordance with 42 U.S.C. Sec. 802; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(2)(b): have been approved by the homelessness council.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The office shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(a): administer the grant program, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(a)(i): reviewing grant applications and making recommendations to the homelessness council; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(a)(ii): distributing grant money to approved grant recipients; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(b): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(b)(i): grant application requirements;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(b)(ii): procedures to approve a grant; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(3)(b)(iii): procedures for distributing money to grant recipients.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4): When reviewing an application for approval, the homelessness council shall consider:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(a): an applicant's rental income plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(b): proposed case management and service plans for households;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(c): any matching funds proposed by an applicant;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(d): proposed restrictions, including deed restrictions, and the duration of restrictions on housing units to facilitate long-term assistance to households;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(e): whether use of funds for the proposed project complies with 42 U.S.C. Sec. 802; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(4)(f): any other considerations as adopted by the council.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-602(5): A grant award under this section shall comply with the requirements of 42 U.S.C. Sec. 802.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(1): "Affected county" means a county of the first, second, third, or fourth class in which a code blue event is anticipated.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(2): "Applicable local homeless council" means the local homeless council that is responsible for coordinating homeless response within an affected county.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(3): "Capacity limit" means a limit as to the number of individuals that a homeless shelter may provide temporary shelter to under a conditional use permit.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(4): 35A-16-702 "Code blue alert" means a proclamation issued by the Department of Health and Human Services under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(5): 35A-16-702(4) "Code blue event" means a weather event in which the National Weather Service predicts temperatures of 15 degrees Fahrenheit or less, including wind chill, or any other extreme weather conditions established in rules made by the Department of Health and Human Services under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(6): "Homeless shelter" means a facility that provides temporary shelter to individuals experiencing homelessness.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-701(7): "Municipality" means a city, town, or metro township.


Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702 Code blue alert -- Content -- Dissemination -- Rulemaking.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1): The Department of Health and Human Services shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(a): monitor and evaluate forecasts and advisories produced by the National Weather Service;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(b): issue a code blue alert under this section if the Department of Health and Human Services identifies a code blue event; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c): disseminate the code blue alert to:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c)(i): the public at large;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c)(ii): homeless shelters located within an affected county;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c)(iii): local government entities located within an affected county;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c)(iv): the office; and
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(1)(c)(v): any other relevant public or private entities that provide services to individuals experiencing homelessness within an affected county.
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(2): 35A-16-703; (3) The code blue alert shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(2)(a): identify each affected county;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(2)(b): specify the duration of the code blue alert;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(2)(c): 35A-16-703 describe the provisions that take effect for the duration of the code blue alert as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(2)(d): (3) include the information prepared by the office under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(3): (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-702(3)(a): The office shall prepare and regularly update information to assist individuals experiencing homelessness during a code blue event, including:

Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703 Provisions in effect for duration of code blue alert.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Subject to rules made by the Department of Health and Human Services under SubsectionUtah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(1): a homeless shelter may expand the homeless shelter's capacity limit by up to 35% to provide temporary shelter to any number of individuals experiencing homelessness, so long as the homeless shelter is in compliance with the applicable building code and fire code;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(2): a homeless shelter, in coordination with the applicable local homeless council, shall implement expedited intake procedures for individuals experiencing homelessness who request access to the homeless shelter;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(3): (1) a homeless shelter may not deny temporary shelter to any individual experiencing homelessness who requests access to the homeless shelter for temporary shelter unless the homeless shelter is at the capacity limit described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(4): Title 62A, Chapter 2, Licensure of Programs and Facilities any indoor facility owned by a private organization, nonprofit organization, state government entity, or local government entity may be used to provide temporary shelter to individuals experiencing homelessness and is exempt from the licensure requirements of
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(5): homeless shelters, state and local government entities, and other organizations that provide services to individuals experiencing homelessness shall coordinate street outreach efforts to distribute to individuals experiencing homelessness any available resources for survival in cold weather, including clothing items and blankets;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(6): if no beds or other accommodations are available at any homeless shelters located within the affected county, a municipality may not enforce an ordinance that prohibits or abates camping for the duration of the code blue alert and the two days following the day on which the code blue alert ends;
Utah Code Annotated § 35A-16-703(7): a state or local government entity, including a municipality, law enforcement agency, and local health department may not enforce an ordinance or policy to seize from individuals experiencing homelessness any personal items for survival in cold weather, including clothing, blankets, tents, sleeping bags, heaters, stoves, and generators; and
